[2023-11-21][INFO]Ejecutando Query SELECT ROW_NUMBER() OVER (ORDER BY U.puntos DESC) AS 'Posicion', 
                                           U.id as 'id', 
                                           U.usuario, 
                                           U.nivel, 
                                           U.puntos, 
                                           U.foto_perfil, 
                                           U.foto_qr,
                                           COUNT(*) AS 'CantidaddePartidas', 
                                           SUM(P.preguntasContestadas) AS 'CantidaddePreguntas' 
                                            FROM usuario U 
                                            JOIN partida P ON U.id = P.id_usuario 
                                            GROUP BY U.id, U.usuario, U.nivel, U.puntos 
                                            ORDER BY U.puntos DESC
                                            LIMIT 3 OFFSET 0;
